Spent too many hours relaxing at this cafe. They've got every drink you could want as well as a few extras.

There is both indoor and outdoor seating with a few seats that have an ocean view. The only reason I docked a star is because their burritos weren't great. Everything else was fantastic.

Definitely try their avacado toast!<//review>

<user_name>Shon< /user_name><Time>1527919883169<//Time><rate>5< /rate>< Text>
An incredible place for experienced and beginner reptile keepers alike. Their wide selection of snakes, frogs, lizards, invertebrates, and feeder animals never ceases to impress. The animals are in top notch health, and every employee I've spoken to -at both the Long Beach and Garden Grove locations- have been kind, helpful, and very knowledgeable. I wandered into the Long Beach location after hearing from a coworker that they have cheap bedding/ food that I needed for my new leopard gecko. When I walked in, I was simply amazed. It's rare to find such a small shop with everything as well put together as it is in Reptile Factory. Their invertebrates too! All so well taken care of. Many shops tend to neglect their inverts since they're not as "emotive" or "well loved" as other more popular animals, but not Reptile Factory. Beautiful tarantulas, vinegaroons, and other crawlies were active, happy, and comfortable being handled. The prices were fair for what was available too, I'd be happy to spend more for a new animal knowing it was hand raised coming from such an amazing place. After visiting in Long Beach, I had to see their other location, and drove to Garden Grove the same night. Both shops were exemplary. Please consider giving your business to such compassionate animal keepers. They really deserve all the attention they can get.< /Text>

< text>
Decent donut place. Pros: 24 hours, plenty of parking, drive thru, and they press their breakfast sandwiches so they kind of come out tasting like a panini. There's also a little seating area outside with a table and two chairs and some tables on the inside. Cons: it's badly lit (even for a late night donut place) and there's a weird area that just looks messy and sketchy. Probably could do with some better organization and lighting to make it more costumer friendly.<//text>

<text>When I first saw the retirement home behind the restaurant, I thought the food would be bland and the atmosphere would be boring. But to my pleasant surprise the food was bland BUT the salad was amazing. The atmosphere is pretty chill and they like to play Smashing Pumpkins as I sadly eat alone and stare out the window as I reflect on my life's misfortunes and mistakes. Luckily for me, choosing Hill Street was not one of them.

The weekend breakfast specials are fantastic and I admittedly love the chorizo breakfast quesadilla. It's delicious and greasy enough to kill the hangover I have from Friday night after drinking enough Long Island Iced Teas to repress the memories of my father. Never did get those smokes, huh pa?

Customer service is always amazing as well and nobody judges me for silently weeping.

10/10 would have continued to eat here had I not moved up north to find myself.< /text>< user_name>

<Text>Always enjoy lunch in this classic feel coffee shop/diner. Burgers are good, salads are fresh, daily soup is on a rotating schedule and, though I've never gotten it, always gets compliments from those I'm dining with. They've got an extensive breakfast menu, too, if you'd like to satisfy that pancake craving. For lunch, I get the Basil Chicken Pesto sandwich quite often as it is a favorite - fresh grilled chicken breast, melty delicious mozzarella cheese, and a flavorful basil pesto spread all on fresh toasted ciabatta. Maybe not weak-in-the-knees good, but a very good and filling lunch. Service is always consistent and prompt, though a smile with it is hit or miss. Kids eat free all day on Tuesdays.
